[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mSimpleLoggerFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:42[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 03a39a742f79fa3d[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing harness triggered a critical security issue in the Log4j lookup [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism, resulting in a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: Remote JNDI Lookup` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception. The issue indicates that untrusted input can reach `JndiLookup`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing attacker-controlled JNDI lookups against remote URLs, which may lead to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote code execution or data exfiltration depending on the JDK version.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes Log4j’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting pipeline with crafted input.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During message formatting, Log4j’s `StrSubstitutor` resolves lookups via the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Interpolator`, eventually invoking `JndiLookup.lookup`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A call chain in the exception stack:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `JndiLookup.lookup`  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `Interpolator.lookup`  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `StrSubstitutor.resolveVariable` → `substitute` → `replace`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `MessagePatternConverter.format` → `PatternFormatter.format` → [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PatternLayout.toSerializable`  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `AbstractOutputStreamAppender.append` → `LoggerConfig.log` → [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`AbstractLogger.warn`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The raised exception [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m identifies a “Remote JNDI [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLookup” vulnerability, in which attacker-controlled JNDI URLs may be passed to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`InitialContext.lookup`, potentially resulting in:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Loading remote classes for execution  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Disclosure of sensitive information  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The issue arises inside the Log4j core lookup mechanism, not within the harness[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer-provided input flows through Log4j’s substitution engine into the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI lookup.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception is raised by Jazzer’s sanitizer hook [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`NamingContextLookup.kt:[0m[1;36m61[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating detection of an untrusted JNDI operation.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To fully assess the impact, investigate:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The configuration and use of `JndiLookup` and any custom lookup plugins in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup`.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The implementation of `NamingContextLookup` in the Jazzer sanitizer.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The pattern layout definitions and lookup resolution logic in `PatternLayout` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `StrSubstitutor`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any filtering or sanitization layers applied before lookups are invoked.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== Java Exception: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI lookups with attacker-controlled remote URLs can, depending on the JDK[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion, lead to remote code execution or the exfiltration of information.[0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m: * Substitutes variables within a string by values.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m: * This class takes a piece of text and substitutes all the variables within it.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m: * The default definition of a variable is <code>$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mvariableName[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m: * The prefix and suffix can be changed via constructors and set methods.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m: * Variable values are typically resolved from a map, but could also be resolved[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m: * from system properties, or by supplying a custom variable resolver.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m: * The simplest example is to use this class to replace Java System properties. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFor example:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m: * <pre>[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m: * [0m[1;35mStrSubstitutor.replaceSystemProperties[0m[1;39m([0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m: *      [0m[32m"You are running with java.version = $[0m[32m{[0m[32mjava.version[0m[32m}[0m[32m and os.name = [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m$[0m[32m{[0m[32mos.name[0m[32m}[0m[32m."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m: * Typical usage of this class follows the following pattern: First an instance [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis created[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m: * and initialized with the map that contains the values for the available [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m: * If a prefix and/or suffix for variables should be used other than the default[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mones,[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m: * the appropriate settings can be performed. After that the [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m[1;35mreplace[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m: * method can be called passing in the source text for interpolation. In the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturned[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m: * text all variable references [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas long as their values are known[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m: * The following example demonstrates this:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m: * <pre>[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m: * Map valuesMap = [0m[1;35mHashMap[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m: * [0m[1;35mvaluesMap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&quot;animal&quot;, &quot;quick brown fox&quot;[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m: * [0m[1;35mvaluesMap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&quot;target&quot;, &quot;lazy dog&quot;[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m: * String templateString = &quot;The $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39manimal[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m jumped over the $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m.&quot;;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m: * StrSubstitutor sub = new [0m[1;35mStrSubstitutor[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvaluesMap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m: * String resolvedString = [0m[1;35msub.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtemplateString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m: * In addition to this usage pattern there are some static convenience methods [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m: * cover the most common use cases. These methods can be used without the need [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m: * manually creating an instance. However if multiple replace operations are to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m: * performed, creating and reusing an instance of this class will be more [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mefficient.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m: * Variable replacement works in a recursive way. Thus, if a variable value [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontains[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m: * a variable then that variable will also be replaced. Cyclic replacements are[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m: * detected and will cause an exception to be thrown.[0m                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m: * Sometimes the interpolation's result must contain a variable prefix. As an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m: * <pre>[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m: *   The variable $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mname[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m must be used.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m: * Here only the variable's name referred to in the text should be replaced [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m: * in the text [0m[1;39m([0m[39massuming that the value of the <code>name<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m> variable is [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The vulnerability arises because JndiLookup currently allows any JNDI resource [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname containing a colon [0m[1;39m([0m[32m":"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m—including attacker-supplied “ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m…”, “rmi:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m…”, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39metc.—to be passed directly to `InitialContext.lookup`. This enables remote JNDI [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups and leads to critical security issues.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Only `core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeds modification. No harness, fuzzer, test code, or external dependencies are [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtouched.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Key Changes  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Strengthen `[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString jndiName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to reject any name containing a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon‐“java:” scheme.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, skip the JNDI call if `convertJndiName` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns `null` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., disallowed name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Modify `convertJndiName` as follows:  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If `jndiName` is `null`, return `null`.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Find the first colon index: `int colonIdx = [0m[1;35mjndiName.indexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m':'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If `colonIdx >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` *and* the name does *not* start with `[0m[32m"java:"[0m[39m`, treat it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas a disallowed remote scheme and return `null`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Otherwise, if the name has no colon and does not already start with [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"java:comp/env/"[0m[39m`, prefix it with `CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX`.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Return the resulting name.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Amend the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After checking `key == null || !ENABLE_JNDI`, call `[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand store in `String fullName`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If `fullName == null`, immediately return `null`, bypassing [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`InitialContext.lookup`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Example Patch Sketch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno diffs here, for illustration only[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `convertJndiName`:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private String [0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString jndiName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjndiName == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return null;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         int colonIdx = [0m[1;35mjndiName.indexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m':'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Disallow any non-[0m[32m"java:"[0m[39m scheme [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremote URLs[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcolonIdx > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"java:"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return null;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Prefix bare names with container path[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcolonIdx == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m && [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             jndiName = CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX + jndiName;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return jndiName;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before creating the InitialContext:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     String fullName = [0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfullName == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return null;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m proceed: InitialContext ctx = new [0m[1;35mInitialContext[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mctx.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfullName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Behavior  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Local/container lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/[0m[33m...[0m[39m` or bare names like `DataSource`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to work as before.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only remote protocols [0m[1;39m([0m[39mldap, rmi, dns, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are blocked.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `ENABLE_JNDI` flag still governs whether JNDI is globally enabled.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The minimal change confines risk mitigation to `JndiLookup` alone, avoiding [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimpact on other lookup mechanisms or the formatting engine.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No tests or harness code are altered; existing test suites should pass [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors the official CVE-[0m[1;36m2021[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m44228[0m[39m mitigation in later Log4j [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreleases, which restrict JNDI to local contexts only.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users who *intend* to perform remote JNDI lookups will see those lookups [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve to `null`. Documentation should note that non‐“java:” schemes are now [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblocked by default.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If future requirements demand controlled remote JNDI, an explicit API or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystem property should be introduced [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout of scope for this patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to whitelist [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecific protocols/hosts.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The fuzzer triggered a critical security exception due to a remote JNDI lookup in   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Log4j’s JndiLookup class. A preliminary patch was applied to JndiLookup.java that:  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Wrapped the lookup call in a new `convertJndiName` helper.                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Added null checks.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Blocked any JNDI name containing a colon unless it starts with the `java:`        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         prefix.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Preserved the existing container resource path prefix logic.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         After applying the patch, the Log4j Core module fails to compile with multiple      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “class, interface, or enum expected” errors in JndiLookup.java, indicating a likely [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         syntax or brace‐matching problem introduced by the changes.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer fuzzer invocation resulted in                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: Remote JNDI     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Lookup`.                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace pinpoints `JndiLookup.lookup` in `log4j-core`, where an        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attacker-controlled key leads to `[1;35mctx.lookup[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` on an unvalidated name.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Remote JNDI lookups can produce remote code execution or data exfiltration     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         depending on the JDK version.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability occurs entirely within the core Log4j code, not in the       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         fuzzer harness.                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The offending code is in `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup`,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lines around the `lookup` method and its use of `InitialContext.lookup`.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The fuzzer’s minimal input triggered the JNDI branch, confirming control over  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the `key` passed to `lookup`.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In `JndiLookup.java`, the existing `[1;35mlookup[0m[1m([0mString key[1m)[0m` method was augmented:  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • After checking `key == null` or `!ENABLE_JNDI`, call `[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1m([0mkey[1m)[0m`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and return if null.                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Store its result in `fullName` and pass that to `[1;35mctx.lookup[0m[1m([0mfullName[1m)[0m`.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A new private helper `[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1m([0mString jndiName[1m)[0m` was added below the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         existing code. It:                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Returns null if `jndiName` is null.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Finds the first colon; if present and the name does not start with           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[32m"java:"[0m`, returns null [1m([0mdisallowing remote protocols[1m)[0m.                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • If no colon and no container prefix, prepends `[32m"java:comp/env/"[0m`.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Returns the possibly modified name.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - During the Maven rebuild of `log4j-core`, the compiler reports ten errors:     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              class, interface, or enum expected                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              at lines [1;36m78[0m, [1;36m81[0m, [1;36m84[0m, [1;36m86[0m, [1;36m89[0m, [1;36m91[0m, [1;36m93[0m, [1;36m95[0m, [1;36m97[0m, [1;36m99[0m in `JndiLookup.java`.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - These errors typically indicate unmatched braces or misplaced method           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         definitions outside a class block.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The build halts, so no further modules are affected, but the fix is not        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         syntactically valid.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The edited `JndiLookup.java` [1m([0mcore module[1m)[0m should be reviewed for missing or   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extra braces around the modified `lookup` method and the new `convertJndiName`      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         method.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Ensure the placement of the new helper is inside the `JndiLookup` class but    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         outside any other method block.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Verify that `ENABLE_JNDI` and `CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX` remain     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         correctly in scope after the patch.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Check import statements for any new dependencies [1m([0mnone were added, but syntax  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         changes may have shifted class boundaries[1m)[0m.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Confirm the class declaration and closing braces were not inadvertently        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         altered by the patch tooling.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m: * Lookup a String key to a String value.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m: * This class represents the simplest form of a string to string map.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m: * It has a benefit over a map in that it can create the result on[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m: * demand based on the key.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m: * This class comes complete with various factory methods.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m: * If these do not suffice, you can subclass and implement your own matcher.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m: * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m: * @version $Id$[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:public interface StrLookup [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:     * Looks up a String key to a String value.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:     * The internal implementation may use any mechanism to return the value.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:     * The simplest implementation is to use a Map. However, virtually any[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:     * implementation is possible.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:     * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:     * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:     * Or, a numeric based implementation could be created that treats the key[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:     * as an integer, increments the value and return the result as a string -[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:     * converting [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m etc.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:     * The [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link #[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m method always returns a String, regardless of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:     * the underlying data, by converting it as necessary. For example:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:     * <pre>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:     * Map<String, Object> map = new HashMap<String, Object>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35mmap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mInteger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35massertEquals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"2"[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mStrLookup.mapLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmap[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:     * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:     * @param key  the key to be looked up, may be null[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:     * @return the matching value, null if no match[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Identify and correct unmatched braces in `JndiLookup.java`:**  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“class, interface, or enum expected”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m indicate that an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextra closing brace [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was added after the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe last patch. This extra brace closes the class prematurely, causing the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent method definitions to appear outside the class.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the stray `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` introduced by the patch immediately following the `catch`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock of the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method has exactly one opening `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand one matching closing `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Enhance the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method to perform early JNDI‐name [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation:**[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After the existing `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey == null || ! ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check and before the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try` block, insert:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     final String fullName = [0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfullName == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return null;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change the JNDI lookup call to use `fullName` instead of a second call to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mctx.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfullName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This enforces early filtering of disallowed names and avoids redundant [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversions.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Replace the simplistic `convertJndiName` implementation with a robust, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscheme‐aware version:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update the helper to return `null` for `null` input or any non‐`java:` scheme,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprepend the container prefix only when no scheme is present, and otherwise pass [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough valid names:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private String [0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String jndiName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjndiName == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return null;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         final int colonIdx = [0m[1;35mjndiName.indexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m':'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Disallow remote JNDI protocols; only allow [0m[32m"java:"[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcolonIdx > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"java:"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return null;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m No scheme detected: apply container prefix if not already present[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcolonIdx < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX + jndiName;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return jndiName;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This blocks remote JNDI lookups, preserves `java:` schemes, and maintains [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompatibility with container‐prefixed names.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Verify class‐level closing brace remains intact:**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After applying the above edits, ensure there is exactly one final `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` to close[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `public class JndiLookup` definition. No extra or missing braces should remain.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Recompile and validate:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn clean install -pl :log4j-core` to confirm that:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - All syntax errors are resolved.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - No changes to harness, tests, or external dependencies are required.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - The new logic correctly blocks non‐`java:` JNDI names while preserving [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a new unit test [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif missing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to assert that `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"ldap://attacker"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns `null` and that `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"java:comp/env/foo"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` still succeeds when [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ENABLE_JNDI` is `true`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:**  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixing the unmatched braces directly addresses the compilation errors without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering the public API or test code.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introducing an early null‐return for invalid JNDI names enforces the security [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstraint at the method entry point, preventing any opportunity for a remote [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookup call.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The new `convertJndiName` logic is drawn from patterns in `EnvironmentLookup` and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SystemPropertiesLookup`, ensuring consistency in how Log4j handles “lookup” [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplugins.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No harness, fuzzer, or test code is modified, preserving the existing build and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest suites.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By reusing the class‐variable `CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX` and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ENABLE_JNDI`, we avoid adding new dependencies or configuration flags.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential side‐effects are minimal:  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Disallowed JNDI names now return `null` rather than proceeding to a lookup. This [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatches the behavior of other StrLookup implementations on invalid input.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing code paths that relied on non‐`java:` JNDI lookups will now see [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`null`—but given the security risk, this change is intentional and documented.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A follow‐up release note should highlight the tightened JNDI restrictions.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
